	//選報表時,清空日期
	$('#dataclass').change(function(){
 		document.getElementById("datepicker").value = "";
 	});

 		document.getElementById("datepicker").value = "";

    //月報表:只選年月, 年報表:選年
    (function() {
        var orig = $.datepicker._updateDatepicker;
        $.datepicker._updateDatepicker = function(input) {
            var output = orig.call(this, input);
            var datatypeSelect = $('#datatype').val();
                
            if (datatypeSelect=="day") {
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").show();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").show();
            }
            else if (datatypeSelect=="mn" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Hr"){
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").hide();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").show();
            }
            else if (datatypeSelect=="year" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Dy" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Mn"){
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").hide();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").hide();
            }
                
            return output;
        };
    })();
        
 	//日期挑選
	$("#datepicker").datepicker({
	  	showOn: "button",
	  	buttonImage: "images/calendar.gif",
	   	buttonImageOnly: true,
	   	dateFormat:"yy-mm-dd",
	   	changeMonth:true,
	   	changeYear:true,
	   	//minDate: "-3Y",
	   	minDate: "2010-01-01",
	   	maxDate: "-1D",
		showButtonPanel: true,
        showMonthAfterYear: true,
		monthNamesShort: ["01","02","03","04","05","06","07","08","09","10","11","12"],
		dayNamesMin: [ "日","一","二","三","四","五","六" ],
        //月報表:只選年月, 年報表:選年
		onClose: function (dateText, inst) {
       		var datatypeSelect = $('#datatype').val();
       		if (datatypeSelect=="mn" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Hr"){
           	    var year = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-year :selected").val();
				var month = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-month :selected").val();
				$(this).val($.datepicker.formatDate('yy-mm', new Date(year, month, 1)));
           	}
       		else if (datatypeSelect=="year" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Dy" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Mn" ){
           	    var year = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-year :selected").val();
				$(this).val($.datepicker.formatDate('yy', new Date(year, 1, 1)));
       		}
		}
    });
	    
 	//查詢按鈕另開視窗
	$("#doquery").click(function (event){
	  	var st = $("#station option:selected");
	  	var stChName = stList[st.val()][0].trim();
	   	var type = $("#datatype option:selected");	 
	   	var tempurl = "";
	   	var obsItem = "";
	   	if(type.val() == "day"){
	   		tempurl=day_url;
	   	}
	    else if(type.val() == "mn"){
	      	tempurl=mn_url;
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "year"){
	       	tempurl=year_url;
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Hr"){
	       	tempurl=tableHr_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Dy"){
	       	tempurl=tableDy_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Mn"){
	       	tempurl=tableMn_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    
	   	if($("#datepicker").val() != ""){
	   		var url = "";
	   		if(obsItem == ""){
	   		    url=encodeURI(tempurl+"&station="+st.val()+"&stname="+encodeURI(stChName)+"&datepicker="+$("#datepicker").val());
	   		}
	   		else {
	   			url=encodeURI(tempurl+"&station="+st.val()+"&stname="+encodeURI(stChName)+"&obsItem="+obsItem+"&datepicker="+$("#datepicker").val());
	   		}
	   		var windowName = "popUp";          
        	//window.open(url, windowName, "width=1024,height=768,toolbar=yes,menubar=yes,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes");
        	var newWindow = window.open();
        	newWindow.location = url;
        	event.preventDefault();
	   	}
	   	else{
	   		alert("請輸入查詢時間");
	   	}
    });
 	
    function stInfoUpdate(){
    	var st = $("#station option:selected");
    	$.ajax({
			  type: "POST",
			  data: {station_no: st.val()},
			  url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
			  success: function(data) {
				  var stinfo = data.split("|");
				  $("#StationInfo").text(stinfo[0]+" "+stinfo[9]+" ("+stinfo[1]+") ");
				  $("#Longitude").text(stinfo[2]);
				  $("#Latitude").text(stinfo[3]);
				  $("#Altitde").text(stinfo[4]);
				  $("#StnBeginTime").text(stinfo[11]);
				  $("#StnEndTime").text(stinfo[12]);
				  $("#Address").text(stinfo[5]+stinfo[6]);
			  }
		});
    }
    
    //更新下拉式測站的選單與右側地圖
 	function selectedStList(){
 		var stCounty = $("#stationCounty option:selected");
		var i = 0;
		for(var st in stList){
			if( (stList[st][2].trim()==stCounty.val()) && (stList[st][3].trim()=="1")){
				document.stationSelect.station.options[i] = new Option(stList[st][0].trim()+" ("+stList[st][1].trim()+")", st);
				i = i + 1;
			}
			else if( (stList[st][2].trim()==stCounty.val()) && (stList[st][3].trim()=="2")){
				document.stationSelect.station.options[i] = new Option(stList[st][0].trim()+" ("+stList[st][1].trim()+") (撤銷站)", st);
				i = i + 1;
			};
		};
		//document.stationSelect.station.length = Object.keys(stList).length;
		document.stationSelect.station.length = i;
		
		//更換地區地圖
		mapChange(areaList[stCounty.val()]);

 	}
    
    //更新下拉式資料格式的選單
 	function selectedData(){
 		var dataClass = $("#dataclass option:selected");

 		if(dataClass.val() == "purchase"){
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[0] = new Option("逐時降水量月報表 (Hourly Precipitation / month)", "Precp|Hr");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[1] = new Option("逐日降水量年表 (Daily Precipitation / year)", "Precp|Dy");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[2] = new Option("逐月降水量  (Monthly Precipitation / 5 years)", "Precp|Mn");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.length = 3;
 		}
 		else{
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[0] = new Option("日報表 (daily data)", "day");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[1] = new Option("月報表 (monthly data)", "mn");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[2] = new Option("年報表 (yearly data)", "year");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.length = 3;
 		};

 	}
 	

	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
 	$("#stationCounty").change(function (event){
 		selectedStList();
		stInfoUpdate();
 	});

	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
 	$("#dataclass").change(function (event){
 		selectedData();
 	});
 	
	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
    $("#station").change(function (event){
    	stInfoUpdate();
    });

 	$(document).ready(function(){
 		selectedStList();
		stInfoUpdate();
		selectedData();
		mapChange('taiwan');
 	});

 	 	$('.mapdiv').each(function(){
 	 		$(this).mouseover(function(e){
 	 			$.ajax({
 					  type: "POST",
 					  data: {station_no: this.id},
 					  url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
 					  success: function(data) {
 						  var stinfo = data.split("|");
 						  $("#StationInfo").text(stinfo[0]+" "+stinfo[9] +" ("+stinfo[1]+") ");
 						  $("#Longitude").text(stinfo[2]);
 						  $("#Latitude").text(stinfo[3]);
 						  $("#Altitde").text(stinfo[4]);
 						  $("#StnBeginTime").text(stinfo[11]);
 						  $("#Address").text(stinfo[5]+stinfo[6]);
 					  }
 				});		
 	 		}).click(function(){
 	 			$.ajax({
 	 				type: "POST",
 					data: {station_no: this.id},
 					url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
 					success: function(data) {
 						var stinfo = data.split("|");
 			 			$("#stationCounty").val(stinfo[5].trim());
 			 			selectedStList();
 			 			$("#station").val(stinfo[10].trim());
 			 			//$("#station").change();
 					}
 				});
 	 		});
 	 	});
 	
 	}

	//選報表時,清空日期
	$('#dataclass').change(function(){
 		document.getElementById("datepicker").value = "";
 	});
	$('#datatype').change(function(){
 		document.getElementById("datepicker").value = "";
 	});
 		
    //月報表:只選年月, 年報表:選年
    (function() {
        var orig = $.datepicker._updateDatepicker;
        $.datepicker._updateDatepicker = function(input) {
            var output = orig.call(this, input);
            var datatypeSelect = $('#datatype').val();
                
            if (datatypeSelect=="day") {
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").show();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").show();
            }
            else if (datatypeSelect=="mn" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Hr"){
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").hide();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").show();
            }
            else if (datatypeSelect=="year" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Dy" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Mn"){
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").hide();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").hide();
            }
                
            return output;
        };
    })();
        
 	//日期挑選
	$("#datepicker").datepicker({
	  	showOn: "button",
	  	buttonImage: "images/calendar.gif",
	   	buttonImageOnly: true,
	   	dateFormat:"yy-mm-dd",
	   	changeMonth:true,
	   	changeYear:true,
	   	//minDate: "-3Y",
	   	minDate: "2010-01-01",
	   	maxDate: "-1D",
		showButtonPanel: true,
        showMonthAfterYear: true,
		monthNamesShort: ["01","02","03","04","05","06","07","08","09","10","11","12"],
		dayNamesMin: [ "日","一","二","三","四","五","六" ],
        //月報表:只選年月, 年報表:選年
		onClose: function (dateText, inst) {
       		var datatypeSelect = $('#datatype').val();
       		if (datatypeSelect=="mn" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Hr"){
           	    var year = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-year :selected").val();
				var month = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-month :selected").val();
				$(this).val($.datepicker.formatDate('yy-mm', new Date(year, month, 1)));
           	}
       		else if (datatypeSelect=="year" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Dy" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Mn" ){
           	    var year = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-year :selected").val();
				$(this).val($.datepicker.formatDate('yy', new Date(year, 1, 1)));
       		}
		}
    });
	    
 	//查詢按鈕另開視窗
	$("#doquery").click(function (event){
	  	var st = $("#station option:selected");
	  	var stChName = stList[st.val()][0].trim();
	   	var type = $("#datatype option:selected");	 
	   	var tempurl = "";
	   	var obsItem = "";
	   	if(type.val() == "day"){
	   		tempurl=day_url;
	   	}
	    else if(type.val() == "mn"){
	      	tempurl=mn_url;
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "year"){
	       	tempurl=year_url;
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Hr"){
	       	tempurl=tableHr_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Dy"){
	       	tempurl=tableDy_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Mn"){
	       	tempurl=tableMn_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    
	   	if($("#datepicker").val() != ""){
	   		var url = "";
	   		if(obsItem == ""){
	   		    url=encodeURI(tempurl+"&station="+st.val()+"&stname="+encodeURI(stChName)+"&datepicker="+$("#datepicker").val());
	   		}
	   		else {
	   			url=encodeURI(tempurl+"&station="+st.val()+"&stname="+encodeURI(stChName)+"&obsItem="+obsItem+"&datepicker="+$("#datepicker").val());
	   		}
	   		var windowName = "popUp";          
        	//window.open(url, windowName, "width=1024,height=768,toolbar=yes,menubar=yes,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes");
        	var newWindow = window.open();
        	newWindow.location = url;
        	event.preventDefault();
	   	}
	   	else{
	   		alert("請輸入查詢時間");
	   	}
    });
 	
    function stInfoUpdate(){
    	var st = $("#station option:selected");
    	$.ajax({
			  type: "POST",
			  data: {station_no: st.val()},
			  url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
			  success: function(data) {
				  var stinfo = data.split("|");
				  $("#StationInfo").text(stinfo[0]+" "+stinfo[9]+" ("+stinfo[1]+") ");
				  $("#Longitude").text(stinfo[2]);
				  $("#Latitude").text(stinfo[3]);
				  $("#Altitde").text(stinfo[4]);
				  $("#StnBeginTime").text(stinfo[11]);
				  $("#StnEndTime").text(stinfo[12]);
				  $("#Address").text(stinfo[5]+stinfo[6]);
			  }
		});
    }
    
    //更新下拉式測站的選單與右側地圖
 	function selectedStList(){
 		var stCounty = $("#stationCounty option:selected");
		var i = 0;
		for(var st in stList){
			if( (stList[st][2].trim()==stCounty.val()) && (stList[st][3].trim()=="1")){
				document.stationSelect.station.options[i] = new Option(stList[st][0].trim()+" ("+stList[st][1].trim()+")", st);
				i = i + 1;
			}
			else if( (stList[st][2].trim()==stCounty.val()) && (stList[st][3].trim()=="2")){
				document.stationSelect.station.options[i] = new Option(stList[st][0].trim()+" ("+stList[st][1].trim()+") (撤銷站)", st);
				i = i + 1;
			};
		};
		//document.stationSelect.station.length = Object.keys(stList).length;
		document.stationSelect.station.length = i;
		
		//更換地區地圖
		mapChange(areaList[stCounty.val()]);

 	}
    
    //更新下拉式資料格式的選單
 	function selectedData(){
 		var dataClass = $("#dataclass option:selected");

 		if(dataClass.val() == "purchase"){
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[0] = new Option("逐時降水量月報表 (Hourly Precipitation / month)", "Precp|Hr");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[1] = new Option("逐日降水量年表 (Daily Precipitation / year)", "Precp|Dy");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[2] = new Option("逐月降水量  (Monthly Precipitation / 5 years)", "Precp|Mn");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.length = 3;
 		}
 		else{
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[0] = new Option("日報表 (daily data)", "day");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[1] = new Option("月報表 (monthly data)", "mn");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[2] = new Option("年報表 (yearly data)", "year");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.length = 3;
 		};

 	}
 	

	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
 	$("#stationCounty").change(function (event){
 		selectedStList();
		stInfoUpdate();
 	});

	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
 	$("#dataclass").change(function (event){
 		selectedData();
 	});
 	
	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
    $("#station").change(function (event){
    	stInfoUpdate();
    });

 	$(document).ready(function(){
 		selectedStList();
		stInfoUpdate();
		selectedData();
		mapChange('taiwan');
 	});

 	 	$('.mapdiv').each(function(){
 	 		$(this).mouseover(function(e){
 	 			$.ajax({
 					  type: "POST",
 					  data: {station_no: this.id},
 					  url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
 					  success: function(data) {
 						  var stinfo = data.split("|");
 						  $("#StationInfo").text(stinfo[0]+" "+stinfo[9] +" ("+stinfo[1]+") ");
 						  $("#Longitude").text(stinfo[2]);
 						  $("#Latitude").text(stinfo[3]);
 						  $("#Altitde").text(stinfo[4]);
 						  $("#StnBeginTime").text(stinfo[11]);
 						  $("#Address").text(stinfo[5]+stinfo[6]);
 					  }
 				});		
 	 		}).click(function(){
 	 			$.ajax({
 	 				type: "POST",
 					data: {station_no: this.id},
 					url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
 					success: function(data) {
 						var stinfo = data.split("|");
 			 			$("#stationCounty").val(stinfo[5].trim());
 			 			selectedStList();
 			 			$("#station").val(stinfo[10].trim());
 			 			//$("#station").change();
 					}
 				});
 	 		});
 	 	});
 	
 	}


</script></div>

	//選報表時,清空日期
	$('#dataclass').change(function(){
 		document.getElementById("datepicker").value = "";
 	});
	$('#datatype').change(function(){
 		document.getElementById("datepicker").value = "";
 	});
 		
    //月報表:只選年月, 年報表:選年
    (function() {
        var orig = $.datepicker._updateDatepicker;
        $.datepicker._updateDatepicker = function(input) {
            var output = orig.call(this, input);
            var datatypeSelect = $('#datatype').val();
                
            if (datatypeSelect=="day") {
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").show();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").show();
            }
            else if (datatypeSelect=="mn" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Hr"){
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").hide();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").show();
            }
            else if (datatypeSelect=="year" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Dy" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Mn"){
                $(".ui-datepicker-calendar").hide();
                $(".ui-datepicker-month").hide();
            }
                
            return output;
        };
    })();
        
 	//日期挑選
	$("#datepicker").datepicker({
	  	showOn: "button",
	  	buttonImage: "images/calendar.gif",
	   	buttonImageOnly: true,
	   	dateFormat:"yy-mm-dd",
	   	changeMonth:true,
	   	changeYear:true,
	   	//minDate: "-3Y",
	   	minDate: "2010-01-01",
	   	maxDate: "-1D",
		showButtonPanel: true,
        showMonthAfterYear: true,
		monthNamesShort: ["01","02","03","04","05","06","07","08","09","10","11","12"],
		dayNamesMin: [ "日","一","二","三","四","五","六" ],
        //月報表:只選年月, 年報表:選年
		onClose: function (dateText, inst) {
       		var datatypeSelect = $('#datatype').val();
       		if (datatypeSelect=="mn" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Hr"){
           	    var year = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-year :selected").val();
				var month = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-month :selected").val();
				$(this).val($.datepicker.formatDate('yy-mm', new Date(year, month, 1)));
           	}
       		else if (datatypeSelect=="year" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Dy" || datatypeSelect=="Precp|Mn" ){
           	    var year = $("#ui-datepicker-div .ui-datepicker-year :selected").val();
				$(this).val($.datepicker.formatDate('yy', new Date(year, 1, 1)));
       		}
		}
    });
	    
 	//查詢按鈕另開視窗
	$("#doquery").click(function (event){
	  	var st = $("#station option:selected");
	  	var stChName = stList[st.val()][0].trim();
	   	var type = $("#datatype option:selected");	 
	   	var tempurl = "";
	   	var obsItem = "";
	   	if(type.val() == "day"){
	   		tempurl=day_url;
	   	}
	    else if(type.val() == "mn"){
	      	tempurl=mn_url;
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "year"){
	       	tempurl=year_url;
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Hr"){
	       	tempurl=tableHr_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Dy"){
	       	tempurl=tableDy_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    else if(type.val() == "Precp|Mn"){
	       	tempurl=tableMn_url;
	       	//console.log(type.val());
	       	var typeList = type.val().split("|");
	       	obsItem = typeList[0];
	    }
	    
	   	if($("#datepicker").val() != ""){
	   		var url = "";
	   		if(obsItem == ""){
	   		    url=encodeURI(tempurl+"&station="+st.val()+"&stname="+encodeURI(stChName)+"&datepicker="+$("#datepicker").val());
	   		}
	   		else {
	   			url=encodeURI(tempurl+"&station="+st.val()+"&stname="+encodeURI(stChName)+"&obsItem="+obsItem+"&datepicker="+$("#datepicker").val());
	   		}
	   		var windowName = "popUp";          
        	//window.open(url, windowName, "width=1024,height=768,toolbar=yes,menubar=yes,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes");
        	var newWindow = window.open();
        	newWindow.location = url;
        	event.preventDefault();
	   	}
	   	else{
	   		alert("請輸入查詢時間");
	   	}
    });
 	
    function stInfoUpdate(){
    	var st = $("#station option:selected");
    	$.ajax({
			  type: "POST",
			  data: {station_no: st.val()},
			  url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
			  success: function(data) {
				  var stinfo = data.split("|");
				  $("#StationInfo").text(stinfo[0]+" "+stinfo[9]+" ("+stinfo[1]+") ");
				  $("#Longitude").text(stinfo[2]);
				  $("#Latitude").text(stinfo[3]);
				  $("#Altitde").text(stinfo[4]);
				  $("#StnBeginTime").text(stinfo[11]);
				  $("#StnEndTime").text(stinfo[12]);
				  $("#Address").text(stinfo[5]+stinfo[6]);
			  }
		});
    }
    
    //更新下拉式測站的選單與右側地圖
 	function selectedStList(){
 		var stCounty = $("#stationCounty option:selected");
		var i = 0;
		for(var st in stList){
			if( (stList[st][2].trim()==stCounty.val()) && (stList[st][3].trim()=="1")){
				document.stationSelect.station.options[i] = new Option(stList[st][0].trim()+" ("+stList[st][1].trim()+")", st);
				i = i + 1;
			}
			else if( (stList[st][2].trim()==stCounty.val()) && (stList[st][3].trim()=="2")){
				document.stationSelect.station.options[i] = new Option(stList[st][0].trim()+" ("+stList[st][1].trim()+") (撤銷站)", st);
				i = i + 1;
			};
		};
		//document.stationSelect.station.length = Object.keys(stList).length;
		document.stationSelect.station.length = i;
		
		//更換地區地圖
		mapChange(areaList[stCounty.val()]);

 	}
    
    //更新下拉式資料格式的選單
 	function selectedData(){
 		var dataClass = $("#dataclass option:selected");

 		if(dataClass.val() == "purchase"){
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[0] = new Option("逐時降水量月報表 (Hourly Precipitation / month)", "Precp|Hr");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[1] = new Option("逐日降水量年表 (Daily Precipitation / year)", "Precp|Dy");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[2] = new Option("逐月降水量  (Monthly Precipitation / 5 years)", "Precp|Mn");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.length = 3;
 		}
 		else{
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[0] = new Option("日報表 (daily data)", "day");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[1] = new Option("月報表 (monthly data)", "mn");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.options[2] = new Option("年報表 (yearly data)", "year");
 			document.stationSelect.datatype.length = 3;
 		};

 	}
 	

	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
 	$("#stationCounty").change(function (event){
 		selectedStList();
		stInfoUpdate();
 	});

	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
 	$("#dataclass").change(function (event){
 		selectedData();
 	});
 	
	//測站下拉選單 改變底下測站資訊
    $("#station").change(function (event){
    	stInfoUpdate();
    });

 	$(document).ready(function(){
 		selectedStList();
		stInfoUpdate();
		selectedData();
		mapChange('taiwan');
 	});

 	 	$('.mapdiv').each(function(){
 	 		$(this).mouseover(function(e){
 	 			$.ajax({
 					  type: "POST",
 					  data: {station_no: this.id},
 					  url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
 					  success: function(data) {
 						  var stinfo = data.split("|");
 						  $("#StationInfo").text(stinfo[0]+" "+stinfo[9] +" ("+stinfo[1]+") ");
 						  $("#Longitude").text(stinfo[2]);
 						  $("#Latitude").text(stinfo[3]);
 						  $("#Altitde").text(stinfo[4]);
 						  $("#StnBeginTime").text(stinfo[11]);
 						  $("#Address").text(stinfo[5]+stinfo[6]);
 					  }
 				});		
 	 		}).click(function(){
 	 			$.ajax({
 	 				type: "POST",
 					data: {station_no: this.id},
 					url: "QueryDataController.do?command=doQueryStation",
 					success: function(data) {
 						var stinfo = data.split("|");
 			 			$("#stationCounty").val(stinfo[5].trim());
 			 			selectedStList();
 			 			$("#station").val(stinfo[10].trim());
 			 			//$("#station").change();
 					}
 				});
 	 		});
 	 	});
 	
 	}


</script></div>
